			create_real_chinese_imperial_bloodline_effect = yes
			
			narrative_event = { id = soh.5571 } # Inform the world
			
			any_playable_ruler = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						ai = no
						government = chinese_imperial_government
					}
				}
				
				narrative_event = { id = soh.5571 } # Inform the world
			}
		}
	}
}

# Inform the world about the new dynasty
narrative_event = {
	id = soh.5571
	title = EVTTITLE_SOH_5571
	desc = EVTDESC_SOH_5571
	picture = GFX_evt_china_expansionist
	window = EventWindowOffmap
	background = GFX_event_window_news_from_china
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		trigger = {
			character = FROM
		}
		
		name = EVTOPTA_SOH_5571 # An auspicious day!
		
		add_trait = eoc_trait
		
		set_government_type = chinese_imperial_government
		
		hidden_tooltip = {
			mandate_boost_massive_effect = yes
			mandate_boost_massive_effect = yes
		}
		
		update_mandate_modifier_but_ignore_laws_effect = yes
		
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_global_flag = treasure_fleet_is_active
			}
			
			set_global_flag = abort_treasure_fleet_new_dynasty
		}
		
		clean_up_chinese_dynasty_effect = yes
		
		set_up_chinese_dynasty_effect = yes
	}
	
	option = {
		trigger = {
			independent = no
			top_liege = {
				character = FROM
			}
		}
		
		name = EVTOPTB_SOH_5571 # Ten thousand years!
	}
	
	option = {
		trigger = {
			government = chinese_imperial_government
			NOT = {
				character = FROM
			}
		}
		
		name = EVTOPTC_SOH_5571 # I am the true Emperor of China!
		
		hidden_tooltip = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						has_landed_title = e_china
					}
				}
				
				mandate_penalty_massive_effect = yes
			}
		}
		
		update_mandate_modifier_effect = yes
		
		if = {
			limit = {
				e_china = {
					NOR = {
						claimed_by = ROOT
						holder_scope = {
							character = ROOT
						}
					}
				}
			}
			
			e_china = {
				add_weak_pressed_claim = PREV
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		trigger = {
			independent = no
			top_liege = {
				government = chinese_imperial_government
			}
			NOT = {
				character = FROM
			}
		}
		
		name = EVTOPTD_SOH_5571 # Interesting times...
	}
	
	option = {
		trigger = {
			top_liege = {
				NOT = {
					government = chinese_imperial_government
				}
			}
			
			OR = {
				is_within_diplo_range = FROM
				top_liege = {
					any_realm_province = {
						OR = {
							trade_route = silk_road
							region = world_china
							county = {
								de_jure_liege_or_above = e_china
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
		
		name = EVTOPTE_SOH_5571 # This might affect me...
	}
	
	option = {
		trigger = {
			top_liege = {
				NOT = {
					government = chinese_imperial_government
				}
			}
			
			NOR = {
				is_within_diplo_range = FROM
				top_liege = {
					any_realm_province = {
						OR = {
							trade_route = silk_road
							region = world_china
							county = {
								de_jure_liege_or_above = e_china
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
		
		name = EVTOPTF_SOH_5571 # This does not concern me...
	}
}

		if = {
			limit = {

				}

		}
		
		else = {
			clr_character_flag = named_chinese_dynasty
			
			primary_title = {
				set_short_name = no
			}
			
			set_character_flag = new_chinese_imperial_dynasty
			
			create_real_chinese_imperial_bloodline_effect = yes
			
			narrative_event = { id = soh.5573 } # Inform the world
			
			any_playable_ruler = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						ai = no
						government = chinese_imperial_government
					}
				}
				
				narrative_event = { id = soh.5573 } # Inform the world
			}
		}
	}
}

# Inform the world about the new dynasty
narrative_event = {
	id = soh.5573
	title = EVTTITLE_SOH_5573
	desc = EVTDESC_SOH_5573
	picture = GFX_evt_china_expansionist
	window = EventWindowOffmap
	background = GFX_event_window_news_from_china
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		trigger = {
			character = FROM
		}
		
		name = EVTOPTA_SOH_5573 # An auspicious day!
		
		add_trait = eoc_trait
		
		set_government_type = chinese_imperial_government
		
		hidden_tooltip = {
			mandate_boost_massive_effect = yes
			mandate_boost_massive_effect = yes
		}
		
		update_mandate_modifier_but_ignore_laws_effect = yes
		
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_global_flag = treasure_fleet_is_active
			}
			
			set_global_flag = abort_treasure_fleet_new_dynasty
		}
		
		clean_up_chinese_dynasty_effect = yes
		
		set_up_chinese_dynasty_effect = yes
	}
	
	option = {
		trigger = {
			independent = no
			top_liege = {
				character = FROM
			}
		}
		
		name = EVTOPTB_SOH_5573 # Ten thousand years!
	}
	
	option = {
		trigger = {
			government = chinese_imperial_government
			NOT = {
				character = FROM
			}
		}
		
		name = EVTOPTC_SOH_5573 # I am the true Emperor of China!
		
		hidden_tooltip = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						has_landed_title = e_china
					}
				}
				
				mandate_penalty_massive_effect = yes
			}
		}
		
		update_mandate_modifier_effect = yes
		
		if = {
			limit = {
				e_china = {
					NOR = {
						claimed_by = ROOT
						holder_scope = {
							character = ROOT
						}
					}
				}
			}
			
			e_china = {
				add_weak_pressed_claim = PREV
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		trigger = {
			independent = no
			top_liege = {
				government = chinese_imperial_government
			}
			NOT = {
				character = FROM
			}
		}
		
		name = EVTOPTD_SOH_5573 # Interesting times...
	}
	
	option = {
		trigger = {
			top_liege = {
				NOT = {
					government = chinese_imperial_government
				}
			}
			
			OR = {
				is_within_diplo_range = FROM
				top_liege = {
					any_realm_province = {
						OR = {
							trade_route = silk_road
							region = world_china
							county = {
								de_jure_liege_or_above = e_china
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
		
		name = EVTOPTE_SOH_5573 # This might affect me...
	}
	
	option = {
		trigger = {
			top_liege = {
				NOT = {
					government = chinese_imperial_government
				}
			}
			
			NOR = {
				is_within_diplo_range = FROM
				top_liege = {
					any_realm_province = {
						OR = {
							trade_route = silk_road
							region = world_china
							county = {
								de_jure_liege_or_above = e_china
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
		
		name = EVTOPTF_SOH_5573 # This does not concern me...
	}
}

# Same dynasty pretender took over China from CI EoC - keep the dynasty name?
character_event = {
	id = soh.5574
	desc = EVTDESC_SOH_5574
	picture = GFX_evt_china_expansionist
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_diplomacy
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTA_SOH_5574 # I will end the pretender dynasty!
		
		clean_up_chinese_pretender_effect = yes
		
		narrative_event = { id = soh.5575 } # Inform the world
		
		any_playable_ruler = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					ai = no
					government = chinese_imperial_government
					character = event_target:old_emperor_of_china
				}
			}
			
			narrative_event = { id = soh.5575 } # Inform the world
		}
		
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
			
			trigger = {
				NOT = {
					trait = proud
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTB_SOH_5574 # I will keep the pretender dynasty!
		
		copy_pretender_empire_effect = yes
		
		narrative_event = { id = soh.5576 } # Inform the world
		
		any_playable_ruler = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					ai = no
					government = chinese_imperial_government
					character = event_target:old_emperor_of_china
				}
			}
			
			narrative_event = { id = soh.5576 } # Inform the world
		}
		
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
			
			mult_modifier = {
				factor = 0.1
				trait = humble
			}
		}
	}
}

# Inform the world about the same dynasty
narrative_event = {
	id = soh.5575
	title = EVTTITLE_SOH_5575
	desc = EVTDESC_SOH_5575
	picture = GFX_evt_china_expansionist
	window = EventWindowOffmap
	background = GFX_event_window_news_from_china
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		trigger = {
			character = FROM
		}
		
		name = EVTOPTA_SOH_5575 # An auspicious day!
		
		add_trait = eoc_trait
		
		set_government_type = chinese_imperial_government
		
		hidden_tooltip = {
			mandate_boost_massive_effect = yes
		}
		
		update_mandate_modifier_effect = yes
	}
	
	option = {
		trigger = {
			independent = no
			top_liege = {
				character = FROM
			}
			NOT = {
				character = event_target:old_emperor_of_china
			}
		}
		
		name = EVTOPTB_SOH_5575 # Ten thousand years!
	}
	
	option = {
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				AND = {
					government = chinese_imperial_government
					NOT = {
						character = FROM
					}
				}
				character = event_target:old_emperor_of_china
			}
		}
		
		name = EVTOPTC_SOH_5575 # I am the true Emperor of China!
		
		hidden_tooltip = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						has_landed_title = e_china
					}
				}
				
				mandate_penalty_massive_effect = yes
			}
		}
		
		update_mandate_modifier_effect = yes
		
		if = {
			limit = {
				e_china = {
					NOR = {
						claimed_by = ROOT
						holder_scope = {
							character = ROOT
						}
					}
				}
			}
			
			e_china = {
				add_weak_pressed_claim = PREV
			}
		}
		
		if = {
			limit = {
				character = event_target:old_emperor_of_china
			}
			
			save_then_remove_all_mandate_modifiers_effect = yes
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		trigger = {
			independent = no
			top_liege = {
				government = chinese_imperial_government
			}
			NOT = {
				character = FROM
			}
		}
		
		name = EVTOPTD_SOH_5575 # Interesting times...
	}
	
	option = {

				NOT = {
					government = chinese_imperial_government
				}
			}
			
			OR = {
				is_within_diplo_range = FROM
				top_liege = {
					any_realm_province = {
						OR = {
							trade_route = silk_road
							region = world_china
							county = {
								de_jure_liege_or_above = e_china
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
		
		name = EVTOPTE_SOH_5575 # This might affect me...
	}
	
	option = {
		trigger = {
			top_liege = {
				NOT = {
					government = chinese_imperial_government
				}
			}
			
			NOR = {
				is_within_diplo_range = FROM
				top_liege = {
					any_realm_province = {
						OR = {
							trade_route = silk_road
							region = world_china
							county = {
								de_jure_liege_or_above = e_china
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
		
		name = EVTOPTF_SOH_5575 # This does not concern me...

}

								de_jure_liege_or_above = e_china
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
		
		name = EVTOPTF_SOH_5576 # This does not concern me...
	}
}

# Inform the world about the new dynasty
narrative_event = {
	id = soh.5578
	title = EVTTITLE_SOH_5578
	desc = EVTDESC_SOH_5578
	picture = GFX_evt_china_expansionist
	window = EventWindowOffmap
	background = GFX_event_window_news_from_china
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		trigger = {
			character = FROM
		}
		
		name = EVTOPTA_SOH_5578 # An auspicious day!
		
		add_trait = eoc_trait
		
		set_government_type = chinese_imperial_government
		
		hidden_tooltip = {
			mandate_boost_massive_effect = yes
			mandate_boost_massive_effect = yes
		}
		
		update_mandate_modifier_but_ignore_laws_effect = yes
		
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_global_flag = treasure_fleet_is_active
			}
			
			set_global_flag = abort_treasure_fleet_new_dynasty
		}
		
		clean_up_chinese_dynasty_effect = yes
		
		set_up_chinese_dynasty_effect = yes
	}
	
	option = {
		trigger = {
			independent = no
			top_liege = {
				character = FROM
			}
		}
		
		name = EVTOPTB_SOH_5578 # Ten thousand years!
	}
	
	option = {
		trigger = {
			government = chinese_imperial_government
			NOT = {
				character = FROM
			}
		}
		
		name = EVTOPTC_SOH_5578 # I am the true Emperor of China!
		
		hidden_tooltip = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						has_landed_title = e_china
					}
				}
				
				mandate_penalty_massive_effect = yes
			}
		}
		
		update_mandate_modifier_effect = yes
		
		if = {
			limit = {
				e_china = {
					NOR = {
						claimed_by = ROOT
						holder_scope = {
							character = ROOT
						}
					}
				}
			}
			
			e_china = {
				add_weak_pressed_claim = PREV
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		trigger = {
			independent = no
			top_liege = {
				government = chinese_imperial_government
			}
			NOT = {
				character = FROM
			}
		}
		
		name = EVTOPTD_SOH_5578 # Interesting times...
	}
	
	option = {
		trigger = {
			top_liege = {
				NOT = {
					government = chinese_imperial_government
				}
			}
			
			OR = {
				is_within_diplo_range = FROM
				top_liege = {
					any_realm_province = {
						OR = {
							trade_route = silk_road
							region = world_china
							county = {
								de_jure_liege_or_above = e_china
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
		
		name = EVTOPTE_SOH_5578 # This might affect me...
	}
	
	option = {
		trigger = {
			top_liege = {
				NOT = {
					government = chinese_imperial_government
				}
			}
			
			NOR = {
				is_within_diplo_range = FROM
				top_liege = {
					any_realm_province = {
						OR = {
							trade_route = silk_road
							region = world_china
							county = {
								de_jure_liege_or_above = e_china
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
		
		name = EVTOPTF_SOH_5578 # This does not concern me...
	}
}

# Inform the world about the new dynasty
narrative_event = {
	id = soh.5580
	title = EVTTITLE_SOH_5580
	desc = EVTDESC_SOH_5580
	picture = GFX_evt_china_expansionist
	window = EventWindowOffmap
	background = GFX_event_window_news_from_china
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		trigger = {
			character = FROM
		}
		
		name = EVTOPTA_SOH_5580 # An auspicious day!
		
		add_trait = eoc_trait
		
		set_government_type = chinese_imperial_government
		
		hidden_tooltip = {
			mandate_boost_massive_effect = yes
			mandate_boost_massive_effect = yes
		}
		
		update_mandate_modifier_but_ignore_laws_effect = yes
		
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_global_flag = treasure_fleet_is_active
			}
			
			set_global_flag = abort_treasure_fleet_new_dynasty
		}
		
		clean_up_chinese_dynasty_effect = yes
		
		set_up_chinese_dynasty_effect = yes
	}
	
	option = {
		trigger = {
			independent = no
			top_liege = {
				character = FROM
			}
			NOT = {
				character = event_target:old_emperor_of_china
			}
		}
		
		name = EVTOPTB_SOH_5580 # Ten thousand years!
	}
	
	option = {
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				AND = {
					government = chinese_imperial_government
					NOT = {
						character = FROM
					}
				}
				character = event_target:old_emperor_of_china
			}
		}
		
		name = EVTOPTC_SOH_5580 # I am the true Emperor of China!
		
		hidden_tooltip = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						has_landed_title = e_china
					}
				}
				
				mandate_penalty_massive_effect = yes
			}
		}
		
		update_mandate_modifier_effect = yes
		
		if = {
			limit = {
				e_china = {
					NOR = {
						claimed_by = ROOT
						holder_scope = {
							character = ROOT
						}
					}
				}
			}
			e_china = {
				add_weak_pressed_claim = PREV
			}
		}
		
		if = {
			limit = {
				character = event_target:old_emperor_of_china
			}
			
			save_then_remove_all_mandate_modifiers_effect = yes
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		trigger = {
			independent = no
			top_liege = {
				government = chinese_imperial_government
			}
			NOT = {
				character = FROM
			}
		}
		
		name = EVTOPTD_SOH_5580 # Interesting times...
	}
	
	option = {
		trigger = {
			top_liege = {
				NOT = {
					government = chinese_imperial_government
				}
			}
			
			OR = {
				is_within_diplo_range = FROM
				top_liege = {
					any_realm_province = {
						OR = {
							trade_route = silk_road
							region = world_china
							county = {
								de_jure_liege_or_above = e_china
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
		
		name = EVTOPTE_SOH_5580 # This might affect me...
	}
	
	option = {
		trigger = {
			top_liege = {
				NOT = {
					government = chinese_imperial_government
				}
			}
			
			NOR = {
				is_within_diplo_range = FROM
				top_liege = {
					any_realm_province = {
						OR = {
							trade_route = silk_road

				set_short_name = no

			create_real_chinese_imperial_bloodline_effect = yes
			
			narrative_event = { id = soh.5582 } # Inform the world
			
			any_playable_ruler = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						ai = no
						government = chinese_imperial_government
						character = event_target:old_emperor_of_china
					}
				}
				
				narrative_event = { id = soh.5582 } # Inform the world
			}
		}
	}
}

# Inform the world about the new dynasty
narrative_event = {
	id = soh.5582
	title = EVTTITLE_SOH_5582
	desc = EVTDESC_SOH_5582
	picture = GFX_evt_china_expansionist
	window = EventWindowOffmap
	background = GFX_event_window_news_from_china
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		trigger = {
			character = FROM
		}
		
		name = EVTOPTA_SOH_5582 # An auspicious day!
		
		add_trait = eoc_trait
		
		set_government_type = chinese_imperial_government
		
		hidden_tooltip = {
			mandate_boost_massive_effect = yes
			mandate_boost_massive_effect = yes
		}
		
		update_mandate_modifier_but_ignore_laws_effect = yes
		
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_global_flag = treasure_fleet_is_active
			}
			
			set_global_flag = abort_treasure_fleet_new_dynasty
		}
		
		clean_up_chinese_dynasty_effect = yes
		
		set_up_chinese_dynasty_effect = yes
	}
	
	option = {
		trigger = {
			independent = no
			top_liege = {
				character = FROM
			}
			NOT = {
				character = event_target:old_emperor_of_china
			}
		}
		
		name = EVTOPTB_SOH_5582 # Ten thousand years!
	}
	
	option = {
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				AND = {
					government = chinese_imperial_government
					NOT = {
						character = FROM
					}
				}
				character = event_target:old_emperor_of_china
			}
		}
		
		name = EVTOPTC_SOH_5582 # I am the true Emperor of China!
		
		hidden_tooltip = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						has_landed_title = e_china
					}
				}
				
				mandate_penalty_massive_effect = yes
			}
		}
		
		update_mandate_modifier_effect = yes
		
		if = {
			limit = {
				e_china = {
					NOR = {
						claimed_by = ROOT
						holder_scope = {
							character = ROOT
						}
					}
				}
			}
			e_china = {
				add_weak_pressed_claim = PREV
			}
		}
		
		if = {
			limit = {
				character = event_target:old_emperor_of_china
			}
			
			save_then_remove_all_mandate_modifiers_effect = yes
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		trigger = {
			independent = no
			top_liege = {
				government = chinese_imperial_government
			}
			NOT = {
				character = FROM
			}
		}
		
		name = EVTOPTD_SOH_5582 # Interesting times...
	}
	
	option = {
		trigger = {
			top_liege = {
				NOT = {
					government = chinese_imperial_government
				}
			}
			
			OR = {
				is_within_diplo_range = FROM
				top_liege = {
					any_realm_province = {
						OR = {
							trade_route = silk_road
							region = world_china
							county = {
								de_jure_liege_or_above = e_china
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
		
		name = EVTOPTE_SOH_5582 # This might affect me...
	}
	
	option = {
		trigger = {
			top_liege = {
				NOT = {
					government = chinese_imperial_government
				}
			}
			
			NOR = {
				is_within_diplo_range = FROM
				top_liege = {
					any_realm_province = {
						OR = {
							trade_route = silk_road
							region = world_china
							county = {
								de_jure_liege_or_above = e_china
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
		
		name = EVTOPTF_SOH_5582 # This does not concern me...
	}
}

			clr_character_flag = named_chinese_dynasty

				set_short_name = no
			}
			
			set_character_flag = new_chinese_imperial_dynasty

			any_playable_ruler = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						ai = no
						government = chinese_imperial_government
						character = event_target:old_emperor_of_china
					}
				}
				
				narrative_event = { id = soh.5584 } # Inform the world
			}
		}
	}
}

# Inform the world about the new dynasty
narrative_event = {
	id = soh.5584
	title = EVTTITLE_SOH_5584
	desc = EVTDESC_SOH_5584
	picture = GFX_evt_china_expansionist
	window = EventWindowOffmap
	background = GFX_event_window_news_from_china
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		trigger = {
			character = FROM
		}
		
		name = EVTOPTA_SOH_5584 # An auspicious day!
		
		add_trait = eoc_trait
		
		set_government_type = chinese_imperial_government
		
		hidden_tooltip = {
			mandate_boost_massive_effect = yes
			mandate_boost_massive_effect = yes
		}
		
		update_mandate_modifier_but_ignore_laws_effect = yes
		
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_global_flag = treasure_fleet_is_active
			}
			
			set_global_flag = abort_treasure_fleet_new_dynasty
		}
		
		clean_up_chinese_dynasty_effect = yes
		
		set_up_chinese_dynasty_effect = yes
	}
	
	option = {
		trigger = {
			independent = no
			top_liege = {
				character = FROM
			}
			NOT = {
				character = event_target:old_emperor_of_china
			}
		}
		
		name = EVTOPTB_SOH_5584 # Ten thousand years!
	}
	
	option = {
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				AND = {
					government = chinese_imperial_government
					NOT = {
						character = FROM
					}
				}
				character = event_target:old_emperor_of_china
			}
		}
		
		name = EVTOPTC_SOH_5584 # I am the true Emperor of China!
		
		hidden_tooltip = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						has_landed_title = e_china
					}
				}
				
				mandate_penalty_massive_effect = yes
			}
		}
		
		update_mandate_modifier_effect = yes
		
		if = {
			limit = {
				e_china = {
					NOR = {
						claimed_by = ROOT
						holder_scope = {
							character = ROOT
						}
					}
				}
			}
			e_china = {
				add_weak_pressed_claim = PREV
			}
		}
		
		if = {
			limit = {
				character = event_target:old_emperor_of_china
			}
			
			save_then_remove_all_mandate_modifiers_effect = yes
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		trigger = {
			independent = no
			top_liege = {
				government = chinese_imperial_government
			}
			NOT = {
				character = FROM
			}
		}
		
		name = EVTOPTD_SOH_5584 # Interesting times...
	}
	
	option = {
		trigger = {
			top_liege = {
				NOT = {
					government = chinese_imperial_government
				}
			}
			
			OR = {
				is_within_diplo_range = FROM
				top_liege = {
					any_realm_province = {
						OR = {
							trade_route = silk_road
							region = world_china
							county = {
								de_jure_liege_or_above = e_china
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
		
		name = EVTOPTE_SOH_5584 # This might affect me...
	}
	
	option = {
		trigger = {
			top_liege = {
				NOT = {
					government = chinese_imperial_government
				}
			}
			
			NOR = {
				is_within_diplo_range = FROM
				top_liege = {
					any_realm_province = {
						OR = {
							trade_route = silk_road
							region = world_china
							county = {
								de_jure_liege_or_above = e_china
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
		
		name = EVTOPTF_SOH_5584 # This does not concern me...
	}
	
	after = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				character = event_target:new_eoc
				event_target:old_emperor_of_china = {
					can_have_chinese_imperial_trigger = yes
				}
				has_game_rule = {
					name = chinese_implosion
					value = allowed
				}
			}
			
			event_target:old_emperor_of_china = {
				character_event = { id = soh.5634 } # Let the interesting times begin!
			}
		}
	}
}



##### Religion/culture conversion affecting status as CI

# Pretender converted culture - no longer Chinese Imperial
character_event = {
	id = soh.5585
	desc = EVTDESC_SOH_5585
	picture = GFX_evt_china_diplomatic_incident
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_diplomacy
	
	is_triggered_only = yes # on_character_convert_culture
	
	only_independent = yes
	
	trigger = {
		tier = emperor
		
		primary_title = {
			has_title_flag = pretender_chinese_empire
		}
		
		FROM = {
			has_chinese_or_historical_culture_for_chinese_imperial_trigger = yes
		}
		
		can_have_chinese_imperial_trigger = no
	}
	
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTA_SOH_5585 # It was not meant to be!
		
		set_character_flag = was_chinese_imperial # Prevents getting cute and getting a bloodline because you convert back
		
		primary_title = {
			save_dynasty_name_effect = yes
		}
		
		clean_up_chinese_pretender_effect = yes
		
		remove_trait = eoc_trait
		
		save_then_remove_all_mandate_modifiers_effect = yes
		
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_feudal = yes
			}
			
			set_correct_feudal_government_type_effect = yes
		}
		
		any_independent_ruler = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					ai = no
					government = chinese_imperial_government
				}
				NOT = {
					character = ROOT
				}
			}
			
			narrative_event = { id = soh.5586 } # Inform the world
		}
	}
}

			has_any_chinese_dynasty_name_trigger = yes
		}
		
		is_feudal = yes
	}
	
	immediate = {
		character_event = { id = soh.5604 } # Destroy other empires
	}
	
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTA_SOH_5596 # Ten thousand years!
		
		set_government_type = chinese_imperial_government
		
		narrative_event = { id = soh.5597 } # Select a dynasty name
	}
}

	after = {

		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					has_character_flag = named_chinese_dynasty
				}
			}
			
			repeat_event = { id = soh.5597 } # Generate new names
		}
		
		else = {
			clr_character_flag = named_chinese_dynasty
			
			primary_title = {
				set_short_name = no
			}
			
			set_character_flag = new_chinese_imperial_dynasty
			
			create_real_chinese_imperial_bloodline_effect = yes
			
			narrative_event = { id = soh.5598 } # Inform the world
			
			any_playable_ruler = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						ai = no
						government = chinese_imperial_government
					}
				}
				
				narrative_event = { id = soh.5598 } # Inform the world
			}
		}
	}
}

# Inform the world - China is now CI
narrative_event = {
	id = soh.5598
	title = EVTTITLE_SOH_5598
	desc = EVTDESC_SOH_5598
	picture = GFX_evt_china_golden_age
	window = EventWindowOffmap
	background = GFX_event_window_news_from_china
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		trigger = {
			character = FROM
		}
		
		name = EVTOPTA_SOH_5598 # An auspicious day!
		
		add_trait = eoc_trait
		
		set_government_type = chinese_imperial_government
		
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					has_character_flag = was_chinese_imperial
				}
			}
			
			mandate_boost_massive_effect = yes
			mandate_boost_massive_effect = yes
		}
		
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					has_character_flag = was_chinese_imperial
				}
			}
			
			update_mandate_modifier_but_ignore_laws_effect = yes
		}
		
		else = {
			update_mandate_modifier_effect = yes
		}
		
		clean_up_chinese_dynasty_effect = yes
		
		set_up_chinese_dynasty_effect = yes
	}
	
	option = {
		trigger = {
			independent = no
			top_liege = {
				character = FROM
			}
		}
		
		name = EVTOPTB_SOH_5598 # Ten thousand years!
	}
	
	option = {
		trigger = {
			government = chinese_imperial_government
			NOT = {
				character = FROM
			}
		}
		
		name = EVTOPTC_SOH_5598 # I am the true Emperor of China!
		
		hidden_tooltip = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						has_landed_title = e_china
					}
				}
				
				mandate_penalty_massive_effect = yes
			}
		}
		
		update_mandate_modifier_effect = yes
		
		if = {
			limit = {
				e_china = {
					NOR = {
						claimed_by = ROOT
						holder_scope = {
							character = ROOT
						}
					}
				}
			}
			
			e_china = {
				add_weak_pressed_claim = PREV
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		trigger = {
			independent = no
			top_liege = {
				government = chinese_imperial_government
			}
			NOT = {
				character = FROM
			}
		}
		
		name = EVTOPTD_SOH_5598 # Interesting times...
	}
	
	option = {
		trigger = {
			top_liege = {
				NOT = {
					government = chinese_imperial_government
				}
			}
			
			OR = {
				is_within_diplo_range = FROM
				top_liege = {
					any_realm_province = {
						OR = {
							trade_route = silk_road
							region = world_china
							county = {
								de_jure_liege_or_above = e_china
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
		
		name = EVTOPTE_SOH_5598 # This might affect me...
	}
	
	option = {
		trigger = {
			top_liege = {
				NOT = {
					government = chinese_imperial_government
				}
			}
			
			NOR = {
				is_within_diplo_range = FROM
				top_liege = {
					any_realm_province = {
						OR = {
							trade_route = silk_road
							region = world_china
							county = {
								de_jure_liege_or_above = e_china
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
		
		name = EVTOPTF_SOH_5598 # This does not concern me...
	}
}



##### Misc

# Destroy any secondary empires gained by a CI ruler (except China itself) outside special circumstances
character_event = {
	id = soh.5599
	hide_window = yes
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		any_demesne_title = {
			limit = {
				tier = emperor
				is_primary_holder_title = no
				NOT = {
					title = e_china
				}
			}
			
			clear_all_chinese_dynasty_flags_and_update_global_flags_effect = yes
			
			unsafe_destroy_landed_title = THIS
		}
	}
}

# Alternative triggering of soh.5599 from various on_new_holder on_actions
character_event = {
	id = soh.5600
	hide_window = yes
	
	is_triggered_only = yes # on_new_holder/on_new_holder_inheritance/on_new_holder_usurpation
	
	only_independent = yes
	
	trigger = {
		FROM = {
			tier = emperor
			
			NOR = {
				title = e_china
				has_title_flag = pretender_chinese_empire
			}
		}
		
		government = chinese_imperial_government
	}
	
	immediate = {
		character_event = { id = soh.5599 } # Destroy the title
	}
}

# Yearly cleanup of flags and names for titles without holders, also of eoc_trait on the wrong character
character_event = {
	id = soh.5601
	hide_window = yes
	
	is_triggered_only = yes # on_yearly_pulse
	
	only_playable = yes
	
	trigger = {
		owns = event_target:pulse_province
	}
	
	immediate = {
		clean_up_all_chinese_pretenders_effect = yes
		
		any_playable_ruler = {
			limit = {
				trait = eoc_trait
				NOT = {
					government = chinese_imperial_government
				}
			}
			
			save_then_remove_all_mandate_modifiers_effect = yes
			add_trait = former_eoc_trait
		}
	}
}

# Cleanup of dynasty name if non-CI China is taken over by non-CI ruler
character_event = {
	id = soh.5602
	hide_window = yes
	
	is_triggered_only = yes # on_new_holder/on_new_holder_inheritance/on_new_holder_usurpation
	
	only_independent = yes
	
	trigger = {
		FROM = {
			title = e_china
		}
		
		NOT = {
			government = chinese_imperial_government
		}
		
		FROMFROM = {
			can_have_chinese_imperial_trigger = no
		}
		
		e_china = {
			has_any_chinese_dynasty_name_trigger = yes
		}
		
		can_have_chinese_imperial_trigger = no
	}
	
	immediate = {
		clean_up_chinese_dynasty_effect = yes # Clear out Grace and Chinese Princesses
		
		e_china = {
			clear_all_chinese_dynasty_flags_and_update_global_flags_effect = yes
		}
	}
}

# on_startup, add the eoc_trait to all CI rulers
character_event = {
	id = soh.5603
	hide_window = yes
	
	is_triggered_only = yes # on_startup
	
	only_playable = yes
	
	trigger = {
		owns = event_target:pulse_province
		NOT = {
			has_global_flag = eoc_trait_added
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		set_global_flag = eoc_trait_added
		
		any_independent_ruler = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					primary_title = { has_title_flag = pretender_chinese_empire }
					has_landed_title = e_china
					government = chinese_imperial_government
				}
			}
			
			set_government_type = chinese_imperial_government
			
			primary_title = {
				update_global_china_flags_effect = yes # Make sure dynasties are properly tracked
			}
			
			trigger_switch = {
				on_trigger = has_character_flag
				
				moh_1 = {
					remove_character_modifier = mandate_of_heaven_5
					remove_character_modifier = mandate_of_heaven_4
					remove_character_modifier = mandate_of_heaven_3
					remove_character_modifier = mandate_of_heaven_2
					remove_character_modifier = mandate_of_heaven_1
					
					add_character_modifier = {
						modifier = mandate_of_heaven_1
						duration = -1
					}
					
					set_variable = {
						which = mandate_of_heaven
						value = -90
					}
					
					set_character_flag = historical_starting_mandate_set
					
					clr_character_flag = moh_1
					
					#log = "[This.GetBestName]'s Mandate of Heaven rating is Lost!"
				}
				
				moh_2 = {
					remove_character_modifier = mandate_of_heaven_5
					remove_character_modifier = mandate_of_heaven_4
					remove_character_modifier = mandate_of_heaven_3
					remove_character_modifier = mandate_of_heaven_2
					remove_character_modifier = mandate_of_heaven_1
					
					add_character_modifier = {
						modifier = mandate_of_heaven_2
						duration = -1
					}
					
					set_variable = {
						which = mandate_of_heaven
						value = -50
					}
					
					set_character_flag = historical_starting_mandate_set
					
					clr_character_flag = moh_2
					
					#log = "[This.GetBestName]'s Mandate of Heaven rating is Poor!"
				}
				
				moh_3 = {
				remove_character_modifier = mandate_of_heaven_5
					remove_character_modifier = mandate_of_heaven_4
					remove_character_modifier = mandate_of_heaven_3
					remove_character_modifier = mandate_of_heaven_2
					remove_character_modifier = mandate_of_heaven_1
					
					add_character_modifier = {
						modifier = mandate_of_heaven_3
						duration = -1
					}
					
					set_variable = {
						which = mandate_of_heaven
						value = 0
					}
					
					set_character_flag = historical_starting_mandate_set
					
					clr_character_flag = moh_3
					
					#log = "[This.GetBestName]'s Mandate of Heaven rating is Average!"
				}
				
				moh_4 = {
					remove_character_modifier = mandate_of_heaven_5
					remove_character_modifier = mandate_of_heaven_4
					remove_character_modifier = mandate_of_heaven_3
					remove_character_modifier = mandate_of_heaven_2
					remove_character_modifier = mandate_of_heaven_1
					
					add_character_modifier = {
						modifier = mandate_of_heaven_4
						duration = -1
					}
					
					set_variable = {
						which = mandate_of_heaven
						value = 50
					}
					
					set_character_flag = historical_starting_mandate_set
					
					clr_character_flag = moh_4
					
					#log = "[This.GetBestName]'s Mandate of Heaven rating is Good!"
				}
				
				moh_5 = {
					remove_character_modifier = mandate_of_heaven_5
					remove_character_modifier = mandate_of_heaven_4
					remove_character_modifier = mandate_of_heaven_3
					remove_character_modifier = mandate_of_heaven_2
					remove_character_modifier = mandate_of_heaven_1
					
					add_character_modifier = {
						modifier = mandate_of_heaven_5
						duration = -1
					}
					
					set_variable = {
						which = mandate_of_heaven
						value = 90
					}
					
					set_character_flag = historical_starting_mandate_set
					
					clr_character_flag = moh_5
					
					#log = "[This.GetBestName]'s Mandate of Heaven rating is Unquestioned!"
				}
			}
			
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOR = {
						has_character_modifier = mandate_of_heaven_1
						has_character_modifier = mandate_of_heaven_2
						has_character_modifier = mandate_of_heaven_3
						has_character_modifier = mandate_of_heaven_4
						has_character_modifier = mandate_of_heaven_5
					}
				}
				
				set_character_flag = fallback_starting_mandate_set
				
				#log = "[This.GetBestName]'s Mandate of Heaven rating will use the fallback option!"
				
				add_character_modifier = {
					modifier = mandate_of_heaven_3
					duration = -1
				}
					
				set_variable = {
					which = mandate_of_heaven
					value = 0
				}
				
				clr_character_flag = moh_3
			}
			
			add_trait = eoc_trait
			
			character_event = { id = soh.5301 } # Generate starting Court Eunuchs
		}
	}
}

# Clean up extra empires if suddenly Chinese Imperial
character_event = {
	id = soh.5604
	hide_window = yes
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	only_independent = yes
	
	immediate = {
		e_china = {
			make_primary_title = yes
		}
		
		any_demesne_title = {
			limit = {
				tier = emperor
				NOT = {
					title = e_china
				}
			}
			
			unsafe_destroy_landed_title = THIS
			
			add_pressed_claim = PREV
		}
	}
}

# on_death event to set temple names
character_event = {
	id = soh.5605
	hide_window = yes
	
	is_triggered_only = yes # on_death
	
	only_independent = yes
	
	trigger = {
		government = chinese_imperial_government
	}
	
	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					dynasty = 1051151 ### Song Dynasty, known in almost all official artwork as wearing their weird zhangokfutou
					any_owned_bloodline = {
						has_bloodline_flag = song_china # If someone creates a "Song", give them the proper headgear!
					}
				}
			}
			
			add_trait = dead_song_emperor # Complimentary zhangokfutou
		}

		primary_title = { current_heir = { save_event_target_as = target_temple_namer } }
					
		# Historical EoCs (that held e_china) get their historical temple name
		
		trigger_switch = {
			on_trigger = has_character_flag
			
			temple_name_daizong = {
				set_name = "Daizong"
				set_character_flag = temple_name_given
			}
			
			temple_name_dezong = {
				set_name = "Dezong"
				set_character_flag = temple_name_given
			}
			
			temple_name_shunzong = {
				set_name = "Shunzong"
				set_character_flag = temple_name_given
			}
			
			temple_name_xianzong = {
				set_name = "Xianzong"
				set_character_flag = temple_name_given
			}
			
			temple_name_muzong = {
				set_name = "Muzong"
				set_character_flag = temple_name_given
			}
			
			temple_name_jingzong = {
				set_name = "Jingzong"
				set_character_flag = temple_name_given
			}
			
			temple_name_wenzong = {
				set_name = "Wenzong"
				set_character_flag = temple_name_given
			}
			
			temple_name_wuzong = {
				set_name = "Wuzong"
				set_character_flag = temple_name_given
			}
			
			temple_name_xuanzong = {
				set_name = "Xuanzong"
				set_character_flag = temple_name_given
			}
			
			temple_name_yizong = {
				set_name = "Yizong"
				set_character_flag = temple_name_given
			}
			
			temple_name_xiizong = {
				set_name = "Xizong"
				set_character_flag = temple_name_given
			}
			
			temple_name_zhaozong = {
				set_name = "Zhaozong"
				set_character_flag = temple_name_given
			}

				set_name = "Zhaoxuan"
				set_character_flag = temple_name_given
			}
			
			temple_name_taizu = {
				set_name = "Taizu"
				set_character_flag = temple_name_given
			}
			
			temple_name_taizong = {
				set_name = "Taizong"
				set_character_flag = temple_name_given
			}
			
			temple_name_zhenzong = {
				set_name = "Zhenzong"
				set_character_flag = temple_name_given

				set_name = "Renzong"

				set_character_flag = temple_name_given

			}
			
			temple_name_wuzong = {
				set_name = "Wuzong"
				set_character_flag = temple_name_given
			}
			
			temple_name_renzong = {
				set_name = "Renzong"
				set_character_flag = temple_name_given
			}
			
			temple_name_yingzong = {
				set_name = "Yingzong"
				set_character_flag = temple_name_given
			}
			
			temple_name_taiding = {
				set_name = "Taiding"
				set_character_flag = temple_name_given
			}
			
			temple_name_tianshun = {
				set_name = "Tianshun"
				set_character_flag = temple_name_given
			}
			
			temple_name_wenzong = {
				set_name = "Wenzong"
				set_character_flag = temple_name_given
			}
			
			temple_name_mingzong = {
				set_name = "Mingzong"
				set_character_flag = temple_name_given
			}
			
			temple_name_ningzong = {
				set_name = "Ningzong"
				set_character_flag = temple_name_given
			}
			
			temple_name_huizong = {
				set_name = "Huizong"
				set_character_flag = temple_name_given
			}
			
			temple_name_shizong = {
				set_name = "Shizong"
				set_character_flag = temple_name_given
			}
			
			temple_name_xingzong = {
				set_name = "Xingzong"
				set_character_flag = temple_name_given
			}
			
			temple_name_daozong = {
				set_name = "Daozong"
				set_character_flag = temple_name_given
			}
			
			temple_name_tianzuo = {
				set_name = "Tianzuo"
				set_character_flag = temple_name_given
			}
			
			temple_name_kangzong = {
				set_name = "Kangzong"
				set_character_flag = temple_name_given
			}
			
			temple_name_chongzong = {
				set_name = "Chongzong"
				set_character_flag = temple_name_given
			}
			
			temple_name_huanzong = {
				set_name = "Huanzong"
				set_character_flag = temple_name_given
			}
			
			temple_name_xiangzong = {
				set_name = "Xiangzong"
				set_character_flag = temple_name_given
			}
		}
		
		# en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Draft:List_of_temple_names, only names with at least one actually reigning Chinese/pretender emperor (not Korea, not Vietnam) are implemented.
		# Dynasty founders get a dynasty founder temple name
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_character_flag = new_chinese_imperial_dynasty
				NOT = {
					has_character_flag = temple_name_given
				}
			}
			
			random_list = {
				5 = { # By far the most common temple names
					set_name = "Taizu"
				}
				
				5 = { # By far the most common temple names
					set_name = "Gaozu"
				}
				
				1 = { # Not actually a founder, only after end of game
					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 2
						prestige >= 5000
					}
					
					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 2
						prestige >= 12500
					}
					
					set_name = "Chengzu"
				}
				
				1 = {
					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 2
						martial >= 16
					}
					
					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 2
						OR = {
							trait = ambitious
							trait = proud
							trait = zealous
						}
					}
					
					set_name = "Liezu"
				}
				
				1 = { # Not actually a founder, only after end of game
					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 2
						piety >= 2000
					}
					
					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 2
						piety >= 5000
					}
					
					set_name = "Shengzu"
				}
				
				1 = {
					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 3
						father_even_if_dead = { higher_real_tier_than = DUKE }
					}
					
					set_name = "Shizu"
				}
				
				1 = { # Not actually a founder
					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 2
						OR = {
							trait = shy
							personality_traits < 3
						}
					}
					
					set_name = "Suzu"
				}
				
				1 = {
					set_name = "Xianzu"
				}
			}
		}
		
		# Other EoCs (pretenders and otherwise) get a regular temple name
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					has_character_flag = temple_name_given
				}
			}
			
			random_list = {
				1 = { # Explicitly negative
					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 2
						trait = depressed
					}
					
					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 3
						event_target:target_temple_namer = {
							OR = {
								opinion = {
									who = ROOT
									value < -80
								}
								is_rival = ROOT
							}
						}
					}
					
					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 10
						diplomacy < 4
						martial < 4
						stewardship < 4
						intrigue < 4
						learning < 4
					}
					
					set_name = "Aizong"
				}
				
				1 = { # Rare
					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 2
						trait = content
					}
					
					set_name = "Anzong"
				}
				
				2 = { # Uncommon
					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 2
						trait = proud
					}
					
					set_name = "Chengzong"
				}
				
				1 = { # Rare
					set_name = "Chongzong"
				}
				
				2 = { # Uncommon
					set_name = "Daizong"
				}
				
				1 = { # Rare
					set_name = "Daozong"
				}
				
				5 = { # Neutral
					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 2
						piety >= 2000
					}
					
					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 2
						piety >= 5000
					}
					
					set_name = "Dezong"
				}
				
				2 = { # Uncommon
					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 2
						trait = stubborn
					}
					
					set_name = "Dingzong"
				}
				
				1 = { # Rare
					set_name = "Duanzong"
				}
				
				1 = { # Rare
					set_name = "Duzong"
				}
				
				2 = { # Highly respectful
					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 0.1
						diplomacy >= 8
						martial >= 8
						stewardship >= 8
						intrigue >= 8
						learning >= 8
					}
					
					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 2
						prestige >= 5000
					}
					
					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 2
						prestige >= 12500
					}
					
					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 2
						OR = {
							trait = diligent
							trait = ambitious
							trait = just
						}
					}
					
					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 2
						event_target:target_temple_namer = {
							opinion = {
								who = ROOT
								value >= 60
							}
						}
					}
					
					set_name = "Gaozong"
				}
				
				1 = { # Technically not negative, but...
					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 2
						trait = humble
					}
					
					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 5
						diplomacy < 4
						martial < 4
						stewardship < 4
						intrigue < 4
						learning < 4
						event_target:target_temple_namer = {
							opinion = {
								who = ROOT
								value >= 60
							}
						}
					}
					
					set_name = "Gongzong"
				}
				
				2 = { # Uncommon
					set_name = "Guangzong"
				}
				
				1 = { # Rare
					set_name = "Huaizong"
				}
				
				1 = { # Rare
					set_name = "Huanzong"
				}
				
				4 = { # Two uncommon names, both not technically negative, but...
					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 1.5
						trait = kind
					}
					
					set_name = "Huizong"
				}
				
				10 = { # Two names, both neutral
					set_name = "Jingzong"
				}
				
				1 = { # Rare
					set_name = "Kangzong"
				}
				
				2 = { # Uncommon
					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 2
						martial >= 16
					}
					
					mult_modifier = {
						factor = 2
						OR = {
							trait = ambitious
							trait = proud
							trait = zealous
						}
					}
					
					set_name = "Liezong"
				}
				
				1 = { # Rare
					set_name = "Lizong"
				}
				
				2 = { # Uncommon
					set_name = "Mingzong"
				}
				
				1 = { # Rare
					set_name = "Minzong"

##### Mandate of Heaven

# on_yearly_pulse - update the MoH
character_event = {
	id = soh.5607
	hide_window = yes
	
	is_triggered_only = yes # on_yearly_pulse
	
	only_independent = yes
	
	trigger = {
		tier = emperor
		government = chinese_imperial_government
	}
	
	immediate = {
		calculate_mandate_of_heaven_effect = yes
	}
}

# Inform the world - triggered from MoH update
narrative_event = {
	id = soh.5608
	title = EVTTITLE_SOH_5608
	window = EventWindowOffmap
	background = GFX_event_window_news_from_china
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	major = yes
	
	major_trigger = {
		ai = no
		OR = {
			is_within_diplo_range = event_target:mandate_update_character
			top_liege = {
				government = chinese_imperial_government
			}
		}
	}
	
	desc = {
		trigger = {
			event_target:mandate_update_character = {
				has_character_modifier = mandate_of_heaven_5
			}
		}
		text = EVTDESC_SOH_5608_A
		picture = GFX_evt_china_golden_age
	}
	
	desc = {
		trigger = {
			event_target:mandate_update_character = {
				has_character_modifier = mandate_of_heaven_4
			}
		}
		text = EVTDESC_SOH_5608_B
		picture = GFX_evt_chinese_bureaucrat
	}
	
	desc = {
		trigger = {
			event_target:mandate_update_character = {
				has_character_modifier = mandate_of_heaven_3
			}
		}
		text = EVTDESC_SOH_5608_C
		picture = GFX_evt_china_stable
	}
	
	desc = {
		trigger = {
			event_target:mandate_update_character = {
				has_character_modifier = mandate_of_heaven_2
			}
		}
		text = EVTDESC_SOH_5608_D
		picture = GFX_evt_china_unrest
	}
	
	desc = {
		trigger = {
			event_target:mandate_update_character = {
				has_character_modifier = mandate_of_heaven_1
			}
		}
		text = EVTDESC_SOH_5608_E
		picture = GFX_evt_china_civil_war
	}
	
	option = {
		trigger = {
			character = event_target:mandate_update_character
		}
		
		name = EVTOPTA_SOH_5608 # I see...
	}
	
	option = {
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				character = event_target:mandate_update_character
			}
			top_liege = {
				character = event_target:mandate_update_character
			}
		}
		
		name = EVTOPTB_SOH_5608 # I see...
	}
	
	option = {
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				character = event_target:mandate_update_character
			}
			government = chinese_imperial_government
		}
		
		name = EVTOPTC_SOH_5608 # I see...
	}
	
	option = {
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				character = event_target:mandate_update_character
			}
			top_liege = {
				NOT = {
					character = event_target:mandate_update_character
				}
				government = chinese_imperial_government
			}
			independent = no
		}
		
		name = EVTOPTD_SOH_5608 # I see...
	}
	
	option = {
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				character = event_target:mandate_update_character
			}
			top_liege = {
				NOT = {
					government = chinese_imperial_government
				}
				any_realm_province = {
					OR = {
						trade_route = silk_road
						region = world_china
						county = {
							de_jure_liege_or_above = e_china
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
		
		name = EVTOPTE_SOH_5608 # I see...
	}
}

# on_death handling of viceroyalties if the liege has a special succession law
character_event = {
	id = soh.5610
	hide_window = yes
	
	is_triggered_only = yes # on_death
	
	trigger = {
		top_liege = {
			primary_title = {
				OR = {
					has_law = succ_chinese_imperial_succession
					has_law = succ_ma_chu
				}
			}
		}
		
		any_demesne_title = {
			is_vice_royalty = yes
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		top_liege = {
			ROOT = {
				any_demesne_title = {
					limit = {
						is_vice_royalty = yes
						lower_real_tier_than = PREVPREV
					}
					
					set_title_flag = should_change_succession_law
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

# on_new_holder_inheritance handling of the above
character_event = {
	id = soh.5611
	hide_window = yes
	
	is_triggered_only = yes # on_new_holder_inheritance
	
	only_independent = yes

	trigger = {
		FROM = {
			has_title_flag = should_change_succession_law
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		FROM = {
			clr_title_flag = should_change_succession_law
			
			if = {
				limit = {
					ROOT = {
						primary_title = {
							has_law = succ_chinese_imperial_succession
						}
					}
				}
				
				add_law = {
					law = succ_chinese_imperial_succession
					cooldown = no
					opinion_effect = no
				}
			}
			
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					ROOT = {
						primary_title = {
							has_law = succ_ma_chu
						}
					}
				}
				
				add_law = {
					law = succ_ma_chu
					cooldown = no
					opinion_effect = no
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

# Handle titles usurped from vassals on_new_holder_usurpation
character_event = {
	id = soh.5612
	hide_window = yes
	
	is_triggered_only = yes # on_new_holder_usurpation
	
	only_independent = yes

	trigger = {
		real_tier = emperor
		FROM = {
			higher_tier_than = count
		}
		primary_title = {
			OR = {
				has_law = succ_chinese_imperial_succession
				has_law = succ_ma_chu
			}
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		FROM = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					ROOT = {
						primary_title = {
							has_law = succ_chinese_imperial_succession
						}
					}
				}
				
				add_law = {
					law = succ_chinese_imperial_succession
					cooldown = no
					opinion_effect = no
				}
			}
			
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					ROOT = {
						primary_title = {
							has_law = succ_ma_chu
						}
					}
				}
				
				add_law = {
					law = succ_ma_chu
					cooldown = no
					opinion_effect = no
				}
			}
		}
	}
}



##### Handling of non-feudal (is_feudal = no) inheritance/usurpation

# Non-feudal ruler inherited pretender from the same dynasty - ineligible
narrative_event = {
	id = soh.5613
	title = EVTTITLE_SOH_5613
	desc = EVTDESC_SOH_5613
	picture = GFX_evt_china_diplomatic_incident
	window = EventWindowOffmap
	background = GFX_event_window_news_from_china
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTA_SOH_5613 # It was not meant to be!
		
		primary_title = {
			save_dynasty_name_effect = yes
		}
		
		clean_up_chinese_pretender_effect = yes
		
		remove_trait = eoc_trait
		
		save_then_remove_all_mandate_modifiers_effect = yes
		
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_feudal = yes
			}
			
			set_correct_feudal_government_type_effect = yes
		}
		
		any_independent_ruler = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					ai = no
					government = chinese_imperial_government
				}
				NOT = {
					character = ROOT
				}
			}
			
			narrative_event = { id = soh.5614 } # Inform the world
		}
	}
}

			save_dynasty_name_effect = yes
		}

			limit = {
				has_global_flag = treasure_fleet_is_active
			}
			
			set_global_flag = abort_treasure_fleet_china_not_ci
		}
		
		clean_up_chinese_dynasty_effect = yes
		
		clean_up_chinese_pretender_effect = yes
		
		remove_trait = eoc_trait
		
		save_then_remove_all_mandate_modifiers_effect = yes
		
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_feudal = yes
			}
			
			set_correct_feudal_government_type_effect = yes
		}
		
		any_independent_ruler = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					ai = no
					government = chinese_imperial_government
				}
				NOT = {
					character = ROOT
				}
			}

		}
	}

			set_global_flag = abort_treasure_fleet_new_dynasty
		}
		
		clean_up_chinese_dynasty_effect = yes
		
		clean_up_chinese_pretender_effect = yes
		
		remove_trait = eoc_trait
		
		save_then_remove_all_mandate_modifiers_effect = yes
		
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_feudal = yes
			}
			
			set_correct_feudal_government_type_effect = yes
		}
		
		any_independent_ruler = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					ai = no
					government = chinese_imperial_government
				}
				NOT = {
					character = ROOT
				}
			}
			
			narrative_event = { id = soh.5620 } # Inform the world
		}
	}
}

# Became feudal when holding China - China named - EoC
character_event = {
	id = soh.5629
	desc = EVTDESC_SOH_5629
	picture = GFX_evt_china_golden_age
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_diplomacy
	
	is_triggered_only = yes # convert_to_feudalism_indep decision
	
	trigger = {
		e_china = {
			has_any_chinese_dynasty_name_trigger = yes
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		character_event = { id = soh.5604 } # Destroy other empires
	}
	
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTA_SOH_5629 # Ten thousand years!
		
		set_government_type = chinese_imperial_government
		
		narrative_event = { id = soh.5630 } # Inform the world
		
		any_playable_ruler = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					ai = no
					government = chinese_imperial_government
				}
			}
			
			narrative_event = { id = soh.5630 } # Inform the world
		}
	}
}

# Inform the world - China is once more Chinese Imperial
narrative_event = {
	id = soh.5630
	title = EVTTITLE_SOH_5630
	desc = EVTDESC_SOH_5630
	picture = GFX_evt_china_golden_age
	window = EventWindowOffmap
	background = GFX_event_window_news_from_china
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		trigger = {
			character = FROM
		}
		
		name = EVTOPTA_SOH_5630 # An auspicious day!
		
		add_trait = eoc_trait
		
		set_government_type = chinese_imperial_government
		
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					has_character_flag = was_chinese_imperial
				}
			}
			
			mandate_boost_massive_effect = yes
			mandate_boost_massive_effect = yes
		}
		
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					has_character_flag = was_chinese_imperial
				}
			}
			
			update_mandate_modifier_but_ignore_laws_effect = yes
		}
		
		else = {
			update_mandate_modifier_effect = yes
		}
		
		clean_up_chinese_dynasty_effect = yes
		
		set_up_chinese_dynasty_effect = yes
	}
	
	option = {
		trigger = {
			independent = no
			top_liege = {
				character = FROM
			}
		}
		
		name = EVTOPTB_SOH_5630 # Ten thousand years!
	}
	
	option = {
		trigger = {
			government = chinese_imperial_government
			NOT = {
				character = FROM
			}
		}
		
		name = EVTOPTC_SOH_5630 # I am the true Emperor of China!
		
		hidden_tooltip = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						has_landed_title = e_china
					}
				}
				
				mandate_penalty_massive_effect = yes
			}
		}
		
		update_mandate_modifier_effect = yes
		
		if = {
			limit = {
				e_china = {
					NOR = {
						claimed_by = ROOT
						holder_scope = {
							character = ROOT
						}
					}
				}
			}
			
			e_china = {
				add_weak_pressed_claim = PREV
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		trigger = {
			independent = no
			top_liege = {
				government = chinese_imperial_government
			}
			NOT = {
				character = FROM
			}
		}
		
		name = EVTOPTD_SOH_5630 # Interesting times...
	}
	
	option = {
		trigger = {
			top_liege = {
				NOT = {
					government = chinese_imperial_government
				}
			}
			
			OR = {
				is_within_diplo_range = FROM
				top_liege = {
					any_realm_province = {
						OR = {
							trade_route = silk_road
							region = world_china
							county = {
								de_jure_liege_or_above = e_china
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
		
		name = EVTOPTE_SOH_5630 # This might affect me...
	}
	
	option = {
		trigger = {
			top_liege = {
				NOT = {
					government = chinese_imperial_government
				}
			}
			
			NOR = {
				is_within_diplo_range = FROM
				top_liege = {
					any_realm_province = {
						OR = {
							trade_route = silk_road
							region = world_china
							county = {
								de_jure_liege_or_above = e_china
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
		
		name = EVTOPTF_SOH_5630 # This does not concern me...
	}
}

# Inform the world about the new dynasty
narrative_event = {
	id = soh.5633
	title = EVTTITLE_SOH_5633
	desc = EVTDESC_SOH_5633
	picture = GFX_evt_china_golden_age
	window = EventWindowOffmap
	background = GFX_event_window_news_from_china
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		trigger = {
			character = FROM
		}
		
		name = EVTOPTA_SOH_5633 # An auspicious day!
		
		add_trait = eoc_trait
		
		set_government_type = chinese_imperial_government
		
		hidden_tooltip = {
			mandate_boost_massive_effect = yes
			mandate_boost_massive_effect = yes
		}
		
		update_mandate_modifier_but_ignore_laws_effect = yes
		
		clean_up_chinese_dynasty_effect = yes
		
		set_up_chinese_dynasty_effect = yes
	}
	
	option = {
		trigger = {
			independent = no
			top_liege = {
				character = FROM
			}
		}
		
		name = EVTOPTB_SOH_5633 # Ten thousand years!
	}
	
	option = {
		trigger = {
			government = chinese_imperial_government
			NOT = {
				character = FROM
			}
		}
		
		name = EVTOPTC_SOH_5633 # I am the true Emperor of China!
		
		hidden_tooltip = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						has_landed_title = e_china
					}
				}
				
				mandate_penalty_massive_effect = yes
			}
		}
		
		update_mandate_modifier_effect = yes
		
		if = {
			limit = {
				e_china = {
					NOR = {
						claimed_by = ROOT
						holder_scope = {
							character = ROOT
						}
					}
				}
			}
			
			e_china = {
				add_weak_pressed_claim = PREV
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		trigger = {
			independent = no
			top_liege = {
				government = chinese_imperial_government
			}
			NOT = {
				character = FROM
			}
		}
		
		name = EVTOPTD_SOH_5633 # Interesting times...
	}
	
	option = {
		trigger = {
			top_liege = {
				NOT = {
					government = chinese_imperial_government
				}
			}
			
			OR = {
				is_within_diplo_range = FROM
				top_liege = {
					any_realm_province = {
						OR = {
							trade_route = silk_road
							region = world_china
							county = {
								de_jure_liege_or_above = e_china
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
		
		name = EVTOPTE_SOH_5633 # This might affect me...
	}
	
	option = {
		trigger = {
			top_liege = {
				NOT = {
					government = chinese_imperial_government
				}
			}
			
			NOR = {
				is_within_diplo_range = FROM
				top_liege = {
					any_realm_province = {
						OR = {
							trade_route = silk_road
							region = world_china
							county = {
								de_jure_liege_or_above = e_china
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
		
		name = EVTOPTF_SOH_5633 # This does not concern me...
	}
}



##### Special FDaTK-style outcome

# General ideas for the AI logic:
# - Kings never stay vassals of either side unless from the same dynasty and with a suitable culture + religion
# - Rel heads always break free from non-co-religionist liege
# - Former faction backers (check opinion modifiers) side with the guy they backed
# - If not eligible for ConBu or CI, always break free
# - Dynasty members generally side with the dynasty, rarely break free
# - Traits should matter a lot; Ambitious kings should be more likely to claim the Mandate than Content ones, etc.
# - Friends and lovers likely side with friend/lover, rivals likely side against, barring very compelling reasons
# - If the mandate_of_heaven_x modifier of the new EoC is higher than that of the former dynasty, be more likely to side with that, and the other way around
# - Don't side with someone you consider a tyrant
# - Opinion matters; barring compelling reasons, > 50 opinion should probably convince someone to side with that person, < -50 should probably convince someone to side against that person
# - Independence faction members are unlikely to remain vassals

# Hidden setup to determine which version we get
character_event = {
	id = soh.5634
	hide_window = yes
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_feudal = yes
				has_regent = no
				is_inaccessible_or_incapable_trigger = no
				is_adult = yes
				# Capable of ruling
			}
			
			narrative_event = { id = soh.5635 } # Do you want to create a pretender
		}
		
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				any_dynasty_member = {
					higher_tier_than = baron
					
					top_liege = {
						character = event_target:new_eoc
					}
					
					is_playable = yes
					is_feudal = yes
					mercenary = no
					holy_order = no
					has_regent = no
					is_inaccessible_or_incapable_trigger = no
					is_adult = yes
					is_ascetic_trigger = no
					can_have_chinese_imperial_trigger = yes
					# Capable of ruling
				}
			}
			
			character_event = { id = soh.5645 } # See if a dynasty member wishes to create a pretender
		}
		
		else = {
			event_target:new_eoc = {
				character_event = { id = soh.5658 } # See what the realm lords do
			}
		}
	}
}

# Former EoC is still able to govern (not imprisoned/a child/etc.) - do they want to create a pretender?
narrative_event = {
	id = soh.5635
	title = EVTTITLE_SOH_5635
	desc = EVTDESC_SOH_5635
	picture = GFX_evt_china_golden_age
	window = EventWindowOffmap
	background = GFX_event_window_news_from_china
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTA_SOH_5635 # My dynasty is the only legitimate dynasty!
		
		any_realm_lord = {
			limit = {
				higher_tier_than = baron
			}
			any_war = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						attacker = {
							character = PREVPREV
						}
						defender = {
							character = PREVPREV
						}
					}
				}
				
				end_war = invalid # Things can break otherwise...
			}
			
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						i_am_appropriate_regent_trigger = no
					}
				}
				
				set_defacto_liege = event_target:new_eoc
			}
		}
		
		any_war = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					attacker = {
						character = ROOT
					}
					defender = {
						character = ROOT
					}
				}
			}
			
			end_war = invalid # Things can break otherwise...
		}
		
		detract_grace_super_huge_effect = yes
		detract_grace_super_huge_effect = yes
		
		set_defacto_liege = ROOT
		
		give_random_pretender_empire_effect = yes
		
		custom_tooltip = {
			text = continue_same_dynasty
			
			name_pretender_after_old_china_effect = yes
		}
		
		event_target:old_emperor_of_china = {
			opinion = {
				who = ROOT
				modifier = breakaway_pretender
			}
		}
		
		add_trait = eoc_trait
		
		set_government_type = chinese_imperial_government
		
		update_mandate_modifier_effect = yes
		
		any_playable_ruler = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					ai = no
					government = chinese_imperial_government
				}
				OR = {
					character = event_target:new_eoc
					NOT = {
						top_liege = {
							character = event_target:new_eoc
						}
					}
				}
				NOT = {
					character = ROOT
				}
			}
			
			narrative_event = { id = soh.5636 } # Inform the world
		}
		
		event_target:new_eoc = {
			character_event = { id = soh.5637 } # Ping, then go to vassals
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTB_SOH_5635 # I have lost the Mandate of Heaven!
		
		remove_trait = eoc_trait
		
		save_then_remove_all_mandate_modifiers_effect = yes
		
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_feudal = yes
			}
			
			set_correct_feudal_government_type_effect = yes
		}
		
		event_target:new_eoc = {
			character_event = { id = soh.5637 } # Ping, then go to vassals
		}
	}
}

# Former EoC broke away - inform the world

# Ping new EoC
character_event = {
	id = soh.5637
	hide_window = yes
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		any_realm_lord = {
			any_war = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						attacker = {
							character = PREVPREV
						}
						defender = {
							character = PREVPREV
						}
					}
				}
				
				end_war = invalid # Things can break otherwise...
			}
			
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						higher_tier_than = count
						dynasty = event_target:old_emperor_of_china
						NOT = {
							government = chinese_vassal_government
						}
					}
					is_patrician = no
					i_am_appropriate_regent_trigger = no
				}
				
				set_defacto_liege = ROOT # To avoid sub-vassals going with a liege they shouldn't go with
			}
			
			if = {
				limit = {
					is_playable = yes
					OR = {
						higher_tier_than = count
						dynasty = event_target:old_emperor_of_china
						NOT = {
							government = chinese_vassal_government
						}
					}
					has_regent = no
					i_am_appropriate_regent_trigger = no
					OR = {
						is_patrician = no
						is_merchant_republic = yes
					}
				}
				
				narrative_event = { id = soh.5638 } # Make a decision
			}
		}
	}
}

# Remained loyal to the new EoC - inform new EoC
character_event = {
	id = soh.5639
	#desc = EVTDESC_SOH_5639
	#picture = GFX_evt_china_diplomatic_success
	#border = GFX_event_normal_frame_diplomacy
	
	hide_window = yes
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		#name = EVTOPTA_SOH_5639 # Excellent!
		
		if = {
			limit = {
				FROM = {
					tier = king
				}
			}
			
			mandate_boost_large_effect = yes
		}
		
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				FROM = {
					tier = duke
				}
			}
			
			mandate_boost_medium_effect = yes
		}
		
		else = {
			mandate_boost_small_effect = yes
		}
		
		opinion = {
			who = FROM
			modifier = opinion_ci_loyalist
		}
		
		reverse_opinion = {
			who = FROM
			modifier = opinion_ci_i_am_loyalist
		}
	}
}

# Loop over former EoC's dynasty member, as required
character_event = {
	id = soh.5645
	hide_window = yes
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				any_dynasty_member = {
					higher_tier_than = baron
					
					top_liege = {
						character = event_target:new_eoc
					}
					
					is_playable = yes
					is_feudal = yes
					has_regent = no
					mercenary = no
					holy_order = no
					is_inaccessible_or_incapable_trigger = no
					is_adult = yes
					is_ascetic_trigger = no
					can_have_chinese_imperial_trigger = yes
					# Capable of ruling
					
					NOT = {
						has_character_flag = refused_chinese_imperial
					}
				}
			}
			
			random_dynasty_member = {
				limit = {
					higher_tier_than = baron
					
					top_liege = {
						character = event_target:new_eoc
					}
					
					is_playable = yes
					is_feudal = yes
					has_regent = no
					mercenary = no
					holy_order = no
					is_inaccessible_or_incapable_trigger = no
					is_adult = yes
					is_ascetic_trigger = no
					can_have_chinese_imperial_trigger = yes
					# Capable of ruling
					
					NOT = {
						has_character_flag = refused_chinese_imperial
					}
				}
				
				preferred_limit = {
					ROOT = {
						current_heir = {
							character = PREVPREV
						}
					}
				}
				
				preferred_limit = {
					real_tier = king
				}
				
				preferred_limit = {
					real_tier = duke
				}
				
				narrative_event = { id = soh.5646 } # Do you want to keep the dynasty going?
			}
		}
		
		else = {
			any_dynasty_member = {
				clr_character_flag = refused_chinese_imperial
			}
			
			event_target:new_eoc = {
				character_event = { id = soh.5658 } # See what the realm lords do
			}
		}
	}
}

	background = GFX_event_window_news_from_china
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTA_SOH_5646 # My dynasty is the only legitimate dynasty!
		
		any_dynasty_member = {
			clr_character_flag = refused_chinese_imperial
		}
		
		any_realm_lord = {
			limit = {
				higher_tier_than = baron
			}
			
			any_war = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						attacker = {
							character = PREVPREV
						}
						defender = {
							character = PREVPREV
						}
					}
				}
				
				end_war = invalid # Things can break otherwise...
			}
			
			if = {
				limit = {
					i_am_appropriate_regent_trigger = no
				}
				
				set_defacto_liege = event_target:new_eoc
			}
		}
		
		any_war = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					attacker = {
						character = ROOT
					}
					defender = {
						character = ROOT
					}
				}
			}
			
			end_war = invalid # Things can break otherwise...
		}
		
		detract_grace_super_huge_effect = yes
		detract_grace_super_huge_effect = yes
		
		set_defacto_liege = ROOT
		
		save_event_target_as = old_emperor_of_china_heir
		
		give_random_pretender_empire_effect = yes
		
		custom_tooltip = {
			text = continue_same_dynasty
			name_pretender_after_old_china_as_heir_effect = yes
		}
		
		event_target:old_emperor_of_china = {
			opinion = {
				who = ROOT
				modifier = breakaway_pretender
			}
		}
		
		add_trait = eoc_trait
		
		set_government_type = chinese_imperial_government
		
		update_mandate_modifier_effect = yes
		
		any_playable_ruler = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					ai = no
					government = chinese_imperial_government
				}
				OR = {
					character = event_target:new_eoc
					NOT = {
						top_liege = {
							character = event_target:new_eoc
						}
					}
				}
				NOT = {
					character = ROOT
				}
			}
			
			narrative_event = { id = soh.5647 } # Inform the world
		}
		
		event_target:new_eoc = {
			character_event = { id = soh.5648 } # Ping, then go to vassals
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTB_SOH_5646 # We have lost the Mandate of Heaven!
		
		remove_trait = eoc_trait
		
		save_then_remove_all_mandate_modifiers_effect = yes
		
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_feudal = yes
			}
			
			set_correct_feudal_government_type_effect = yes
		}
		
		set_character_flag = refused_chinese_imperial
		
		FROM = {
			character_event = { id = soh.5645 } # Back to the loop
		}
	}
}

# Former EoC's relative broke away - inform the world
narrative_event = {
	id = soh.5647
	title = EVTTITLE_SOH_5647
	desc = EVTDESC_SOH_5647
	picture = GFX_evt_china_civil_war
	window = EventWindowOffmap
	background = GFX_event_window_news_from_china
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		trigger = {
			character = event_target:new_eoc
		}
		
		name = EVTOPTA_SOH_5647 # Your dynasty is already over!
	}
	
	option = {
		trigger = {
			government = chinese_imperial_government
			NOT = {
				character = FROM
			}
			NOT = {
				character = event_target:new_eoc
			}
		}
		
		name = EVTOPTB_SOH_5647 # I am the true Emperor of China!
	}
	
	option = {
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				government = chinese_imperial_government
			}
			
			OR = {
				is_within_diplo_range = FROM
				top_liege = {
					any_realm_province = {
						OR = {
							trade_route = silk_road
							region = world_china
							county = {
								de_jure_liege_or_above = e_china
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
		
		name = EVTOPTC_SOH_5647 # This might affect me...
	}
	
	option = {
		trigger = {
			top_liege = {
				NOT = {
					government = chinese_imperial_government
				}
			}
			
			NOR = {
				is_within_diplo_range = FROM
				top_liege = {
					any_realm_province = {
						OR = {
							trade_route = silk_road
							region = world_china
							county = {
								de_jure_liege_or_above = e_china
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
		
		name = EVTOPTD_SOH_5647 # This does not concern me...
	}
}

# Ping new EoC
character_event = {
	id = soh.5648
	hide_window = yes
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		any_realm_lord = {
			any_war = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						attacker = {
							character = PREVPREV
						}
						defender = {
							character = PREVPREV
						}
					}
				}
				
				end_war = invalid # Things can break otherwise...
			}
			
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						higher_tier_than = count
						dynasty = event_target:old_emperor_of_china
						NOT = {
							government = chinese_vassal_government
						}
					}
					is_patrician = no
					i_am_appropriate_regent_trigger = no
				}
				
				set_defacto_liege = ROOT # To avoid sub-vassals going with a liege they shouldn't go with
			}
			
			if = {
				limit = {
					is_playable = yes
					OR = {
						AND = {
							has_regent = no
							higher_tier_than = count
						}
						dynasty = event_target:old_emperor_of_china_heir
						NOT = {
							government = chinese_vassal_government
						}
					}
					i_am_appropriate_regent_trigger = no
					OR = {
						is_patrician = no
						is_merchant_republic = yes
					}
				}
				
				narrative_event = { id = soh.5649 } # Make a decision
			}
		}
	}
}

			mult_modifier = {
				factor = 10
				real_tier = king
			}
			
			mult_modifier = {
				factor = 10
				trait = proud
			}
			
			mult_modifier = {
				factor = 10
				trait = envious
			}
			
			mult_modifier = {
				factor = 0.01
				trait = humble
			}
			
			mult_modifier = {
				factor = 10
				e_china = {
					claimed_by = ROOT
				}
			}
			
			mult_modifier = {
				factor = 10
				is_rival = event_target:new_eoc
				is_rival = event_target:old_emperor_of_china
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		trigger = {
			character = event_target:old_emperor_of_china
		}
		
		name = EVTOPTE_SOH_5649 # I will give my full support to my heir!
		
		detract_grace_super_huge_effect = yes
		
		abdicate_to = event_target:old_emperor_of_china_heir
		
		add_trait = former_eoc_trait
		
		save_then_remove_all_mandate_modifiers_effect = yes
			
		move_character = event_target:old_emperor_of_china_heir
		
		force_host = event_target:old_emperor_of_china_heir
		
		event_target:new_eoc = {
			character_event = { id = soh.5656 } # Inform EoC
		}
		
		event_target:old_emperor_of_china_heir = {
			character_event = { id = soh.5657 } # Inform former EoC's heir
		}
		
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1000
		}
	}
}

# Ping new EoC
character_event = {
	id = soh.5658
	hide_window = yes
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		any_realm_lord = {
			any_war = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						attacker = {
							character = PREVPREV
						}
						defender = {
							character = PREVPREV
						}
					}
				}
				
				end_war = invalid # Things can break otherwise...
			}
			
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						higher_tier_than = count
						NOT = {
							government = chinese_vassal_government
						}
					}
					is_patrician = no
					i_am_appropriate_regent_trigger = no
				}
				
				set_defacto_liege = ROOT # To avoid sub-vassals going with a liege they shouldn't go with
			}
			
			if = {
				limit = {
					is_playable = yes
					OR = {
						higher_tier_than = count
						NOT = {
							government = chinese_vassal_government
						}
					}
					has_regent = no
					i_am_appropriate_regent_trigger = no
					OR = {
						is_patrician = no
						is_merchant_republic = yes
					}
				}
				
				narrative_event = { id = soh.5659 } # Make a decision
			}
		}
	}
}

# Former dynasty did not continue as a pretender - non-patrician count+ realm lords get to choose between remaining loyal, going independent, or maybe even going pretender (NOT if from the former EoC's dynasty)

	title = EVTTITLE_SOH_5659
	desc = EVTDESC_SOH_5659
	picture = GFX_evt_china_golden_age

	background = GFX_event_window_news_from_china
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				ai = no
				NOT = {
					dynasty = event_target:old_emperor_of_china
				}

			}
		}
		
		name = EVTOPTA_SOH_5659 # I will remain loyal to the new Son/Daughter of Heaven!

		}

			factor = 100

				OR = {

					}

						who = event_target:new_eoc
						modifier = opinion_fought_for_claimant
					}

					religion = event_target:new_eoc
				}

					NOT = {
						is_rival = event_target:new_eoc
					}
				}
				
				OR = {
					dynasty = event_target:new_eoc
					opinion = {
						who = event_target:new_eoc
						value >= -50
					}
				}
				
				NOT = {
					in_faction =  faction_independence
				}
			}

			mult_modifier = {
				factor = 10
				has_opinion_modifier = {
					who = event_target:new_eoc
					modifier = opinion_fought_for_claimant
				}
			}

			mult_modifier = {
				factor = 0.1
				has_opinion_modifier = {

				factor = 100
				dynasty = event_target:new_eoc
				NOT = {
					is_rival = event_target:new_eoc
				}
			}

				factor = 100

					dynasty = event_target:old_emperor_of_china
				}
			}

			mult_modifier = {
				factor = 10
				is_friend = event_target:new_eoc
				dynasty = event_target:old_emperor_of_china
			}

			mult_modifier = {
				factor = 100
				is_lover = event_target:new_eoc
				NOT = {
					dynasty = event_target:old_emperor_of_china
				}
			}

			mult_modifier = {
				factor = 10
				is_lover = event_target:new_eoc
				dynasty = event_target:old_emperor_of_china
			}

			mult_modifier = {
				factor = 5
				event_target:new_eoc = {
					has_character_modifier = mandate_of_heaven_5
				}
			}

			mult_modifier = {
				factor = 2
				event_target:new_eoc = {
					has_character_modifier = mandate_of_heaven_4
				}
			}

			mult_modifier = {
				factor = 0.5
				event_target:new_eoc = {
					has_character_modifier = mandate_of_heaven_2
				}
			}

			mult_modifier = {
				factor = 0.2
				event_target:new_eoc = {
					has_character_modifier = mandate_of_heaven_1
				}
			}

			mult_modifier = {
				factor = 0.1
				opinion = {
					who = event_target:new_eoc
					value < -25
				}
			}

			mult_modifier = {
				factor = 2
				opinion = {
					who = event_target:new_eoc
					value >= 25
				}
			}

			mult_modifier = {
				factor = 5
				opinion = {
					who = event_target:new_eoc
					value >= 50
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {

			OR = {
				ai = no
				NOR = {

			}
		}

		}

			factor = 100

	after = {

		if = {
			limit = {
