		else = {
			clr_character_flag = named_chinese_dynasty
			
			primary_title = {
				set_short_name = no
			}
			
			set_character_flag = new_chinese_imperial_dynasty
			
			create_real_chinese_imperial_bloodline_effect = yes
			
			narrative_event = { id = soh.5663 } # Inform the world
			
			any_playable_ruler = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						ai = no
						government = chinese_imperial_government
					}
				}
				
				narrative_event = { id = soh.5663 } # Inform the world
			}
		}
	}
}

# Inform the world about the new dynasty
narrative_event = {
	id = soh.5663
	title = EVTTITLE_SOH_5663
	desc = EVTDESC_SOH_5663
	picture = GFX_evt_china_expansionist
	window = EventWindowOffmap
	background = GFX_event_window_news_from_china
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		trigger = {
			character = FROM
		}
		
		name = EVTOPTA_SOH_5663 # An auspicious day!
		
		add_trait = eoc_trait
		
		set_government_type = chinese_imperial_government
		
		hidden_tooltip = {
			mandate_boost_massive_effect = yes
			mandate_boost_massive_effect = yes
		}
		
		update_mandate_modifier_but_ignore_laws_effect = yes
		
		clean_up_chinese_dynasty_effect = yes
		
		set_up_chinese_dynasty_effect = yes
	}
	
	option = {
		trigger = {
			independent = no
			top_liege = {
				character = FROM
			}
		}
		
		name = EVTOPTB_SOH_5663 # Ten thousand years!
	}
	
	option = {
		trigger = {
			government = chinese_imperial_government
			NOT = {
				character = FROM
			}
		}
		
		name = EVTOPTC_SOH_5663 # I am the true Emperor of China!
		
		hidden_tooltip = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						has_landed_title = e_china
					}
				}
				
				mandate_penalty_massive_effect = yes
			}
		}
		
		update_mandate_modifier_effect = yes
		
		if = {
			limit = {
				e_china = {
					NOR = {
						claimed_by = ROOT
						holder_scope = {
							character = ROOT
						}
					}
				}
			}
			
			e_china = {
				add_weak_pressed_claim = PREV
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		trigger = {
			independent = no
			top_liege = {
				government = chinese_imperial_government
			}
			NOT = {
				character = FROM
			}
		}
		
		name = EVTOPTD_SOH_5663 # Interesting times...
	}
	
	option = {
		trigger = {
			top_liege = {
				NOT = {
					government = chinese_imperial_government
				}
			}
			
			OR = {
				is_within_diplo_range = FROM
				top_liege = {
					any_realm_province = {
						OR = {
							trade_route = silk_road
							region = world_china
							county = {
								de_jure_liege_or_above = e_china
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
		
		name = EVTOPTE_SOH_5663 # This might affect me...
	}
	
	option = {
		trigger = {
			top_liege = {
				NOT = {
					government = chinese_imperial_government
				}
			}
			
			NOR = {
				is_within_diplo_range = FROM
				top_liege = {
					any_realm_province = {
						OR = {
							trade_route = silk_road
							region = world_china
							county = {
								de_jure_liege_or_above = e_china
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
		
		name = EVTOPTF_SOH_5663 # This does not concern me...
	}
}

##### Misc CI

# Cleanup of Imperial Guard regiments on peace
character_event = {
	id = soh.5664
	hide_window = yes
	
	is_triggered_only = yes # Assorted on_war_ended on_actions
	
	trigger = {
		OR = {
			has_character_modifier = yulin_guard_raised
			has_character_modifier = longwu_guard_raised
			has_character_modifier = shenwu_guard_raised
			has_character_modifier = shence_guard_raised
			has_character_modifier = pengri_guard_raised
			has_character_modifier = tianwu_guard_raised
			has_character_modifier = longwei_guard_raised
			has_character_modifier = shenwei_guard_raised
			has_earmarked_regiments = yulin_guard
			has_earmarked_regiments = longwu_guard
			has_earmarked_regiments = shenwu_guard
			has_earmarked_regiments = shence_guard
			has_earmarked_regiments = pengri_guard
			has_earmarked_regiments = tianwu_guard
			has_earmarked_regiments = longwei_guard
			has_earmarked_regiments = shenwei_guard
			
			
			FROM = {
				OR = {
					has_character_modifier = yulin_guard_raised
					has_character_modifier = longwu_guard_raised
					has_character_modifier = shenwu_guard_raised
					has_character_modifier = shence_guard_raised
					has_character_modifier = pengri_guard_raised
					has_character_modifier = tianwu_guard_raised
					has_character_modifier = longwei_guard_raised
					has_character_modifier = shenwei_guard_raised
					has_earmarked_regiments = yulin_guard
					has_earmarked_regiments = longwu_guard
					has_earmarked_regiments = shenwu_guard
					has_earmarked_regiments = shence_guard
					has_earmarked_regiments = pengri_guard
					has_earmarked_regiments = tianwu_guard
					has_earmarked_regiments = longwei_guard
					has_earmarked_regiments = shenwei_guard
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		ROOT = {
			character_event = {
				id = soh.5665
				days = 1 # One day delay to check for any other wars.
			}
		}
		
		FROM = {
			character_event = {
				id = soh.5665
				days = 1 # One day delay to check for any other wars.
			}
		}
	}
}

# Actual cleanup of Imperial Guard regiments
character_event = {
	id = soh.5665
	hide_window = yes
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	only_playable = yes
	
	trigger = {
		NOT = {
			any_war = {
				OR = {
					attacker = {
						character = ROOT
					}
					defender = {
						character = ROOT
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		disband_event_forces = yulin_guard
		disband_event_forces = longwu_guard
		disband_event_forces = shenwu_guard
		disband_event_forces = shence_guard
		disband_event_forces = pengri_guard
		disband_event_forces = tianwu_guard
		disband_event_forces = longwei_guard
		disband_event_forces = shenwei_guard
		
		remove_character_modifier = yulin_guard_raised
		remove_character_modifier = longwu_guard_raised
		remove_character_modifier = shenwu_guard_raised
		remove_character_modifier = shence_guard_raised
		remove_character_modifier = pengri_guard_raised
		remove_character_modifier = tianwu_guard_raised
		remove_character_modifier = longwei_guard_raised
		remove_character_modifier = shenwei_guard_raised
	}
}

# Handling of CI rulers (at least of China) sometimes going way above their demesne limit and not understanding what to do
character_event = {
	id = soh.5666
	hide_window = yes
	
	is_triggered_only = yes # on_new_holder/on_new_holder_inheritance/on_new_holder_usurpation
	
	only_independent = yes
	ai = yes
	
	trigger = {
		government = chinese_imperial_government
		over_max_demesne_size >= 2
		FROM = {
			OR = {
				tier = count
				tier = baron
			}
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		# Pick a suitable title
		random_demesne_title = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					tier = baron
					tier = count
				}
				NOT = {
					ROOT = {
						capital_scope = {
							county = {
								title = PREVPREVPREV
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
			
			preferred_limit = {
				tier = baron
			}
			
			preferred_limit = {
				NOT = {
					de_jure_liege_or_above = ROOT
				}
			}
			
			save_event_target_as = title_to_give_away
		}
		# Hand the title to someone suitable
		if = {
			limit = {
				any_courtier = {
					same_sex = ROOT # Probably good enough
					is_adult = yes
					prisoner = no
					is_ascetic_trigger = no
				}
			}
			
			random_courtier = {
				limit = {
					same_sex = ROOT # Probably good enough
					is_adult = yes
					prisoner = no
				}
				
				preferred_limit = {
					culture = ROOT
					religion = ROOT
				}
				
				preferred_limit = {
					could_have_chinese_government_trigger = yes
				}
				
				grant_title = event_target:title_to_give_away
			}
		}
		
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				any_realm_lord = {
					any_courtier = {
						same_sex = ROOT # Probably good enough
						is_adult = yes
						prisoner = no
						is_ascetic_trigger = no
					}
				}
			}
			
			random_realm_lord = {
				limit = {
					any_courtier = {
						same_sex = ROOT # Probably good enough
						is_adult = yes
						prisoner = no
						is_ascetic_trigger = no
					}
				}
				
				random_courtier = {
					limit = {
						same_sex = ROOT # Probably good enough
						is_adult = yes
						prisoner = no
					}
					
					preferred_limit = {
						culture = ROOT
						religion = ROOT
					}
					
					preferred_limit = {
						could_have_chinese_government_trigger = yes
					}
					
					grant_title = event_target:title_to_give_away
				}
			}
		}
		
		else = {
			create_character = {
				age = 30
				dynasty = culture
				culture = ROOT
				religion = ROOT
				is_female = no
				random_traits = yes
			}
			
			new_character = {
				grant_title = event_target:title_to_give_away
			}
		}
	}
}

# Handling of dynasty members being where they shouldn't be
character_event = {
	id = soh.5667
	hide_window = yes
	
	is_triggered_only = yes # on_startup
	
	only_playable = yes
	
	trigger = {
		owns = event_target:pulse_province
		NOT = {
			has_global_flag = courtiers_moved
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		set_global_flag = courtiers_moved
		
		any_independent_ruler = {
			limit = {
				government = chinese_imperial_government
			}
			
			character_event = { id = soh.5668 } # Fire the event for CI rulers
		}
		
		k_chrysanthemum_throne = {
			holder_scope = {
				character_event = { id = soh.5668 } # Fire the event for CI rulers
			}
		}
	}
}

# Actual event
character_event = {
	id = soh.5668
	hide_window = yes
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		any_dynasty_member = {
			limit = {
				is_landed = no
				prisoner = no
				employer = {
					NOR = {
						character = ROOT
						is_close_relative = PREV
						is_consort =  PREV
						any_close_relative = {
							employer = {
								character = PREV
							}
							OR = {
								is_married = PREVPREV
								is_consort = PREVPREV
							}
						}
						is_descendant_of = PREV
					}
				}
			}
			
			move_character = ROOT
			force_host = ROOT
		}
		
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_chinese_emperor_trigger = yes
			}
			
			set_up_chinese_dynasty_effect = yes
		}
	}
}

# Capital moves for the AI
character_event = {
	id = soh.5669
	hide_window = yes
	
	is_triggered_only = yes # on_decade_pulse
	
	only_independent = yes
	war = no
	prisoner = no
	min_age = 16
	ai = yes
	
	trigger = {
		is_chinese_emperor_trigger = yes
		is_inaccessible_or_incapable_trigger = no
		NOT = {
			has_character_flag = moved_chinas_capital
		}
		
		trigger_if = {
			limit = {
				dynasty = 11100 # Borjigin (Yuan)
			}
			e_china = {
				capital_scope = {
					county = {
						NOT = {
							title = c_dadu
						}
					}
				}
			}
			any_realm_province = {
				county = {
					title = c_dadu
				}
			}
		}
		
		trigger_else_if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					dynasty = 1051150 # Li (Tang)
					dynasty = 1045082 # Yelü
				}
			}
			OR = {
				AND = {
					e_china = {
						capital_scope = {
							county = {
								NOT = {
									title = c_changan
								}
							}
						}
					}

				}
			}

		set_character_flag = moved_chinas_capital
		
		wealth = -1000

					}
				}
			}

						}
					}
				}
				
				else = {

						e_china = {
							set_preferred_capital = PREV
						}
					}
				}
			}
			
			1045082 = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						any_realm_province = {
							county = {

							}
